</span></span>\n}}\nThis absolutely delicious version of [[Singapore noodles]] uses two [[Air Fryers|air fryers]] although you could probably make this recipe in one air fryer or even in a large [[Wok|wok]].\n\nThe beauty of using the two [[Air Fryers|air fryers]] is that once the ingredients are prepared, there is almost nothing else to do during the cooking cycle.\n\nWe currently have an [[Tefal Actifry Genius]] air fryer, the rotating paddle type and also a [[Pro Breeze XL 5.5L Air Fryer]] which is like a small fan-assisted oven (5.5 litres).\n\nI have used the paddle [[Air Fryer|air fryer]] to '[[Stir-fry|stir-fry]]' the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and the fan-[[Oven|oven]] [[Air fryer|air fryer]] to cook the [[Marinated|marinated]] [[Meat|meat]].  When everything is almost done, everything is added together in the large fan [[Air-fryer|air-fryer]], mix together and the [[Noodle|noodle]] and [[Bean sprouts|bean sprouts]] are added and cooked for the last few minutes.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====Vegetable mix====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 125g sliced [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 medium [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], cored and chopped into strips\n| 1 large [[Courgette|courgette]] cut into slices\n| 2 tablespoons [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 2 thumb-sized pieces of ginger, cut into thin slices - no need to peel the ginger!\n}}\n====Chicken and marinade====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 large [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]] cut into bite-sized pieces\n| 2 tablespoons [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Demerara sugar|demerara sugar]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 1 heaped teaspoon of [[Curry powder|curry powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Turmeric|turmeric]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coriander|coriander]] whole [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| A pinch of whole [[Fenugreek seeds|fenugreek seeds]]\n| A good pinch of [[5 spice powder]]\n| 4 [[Fat|fat]] [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n}}\n====Noodles and beanshoots====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 200g pre-cooked [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]]\n| 125g [[Bean|bean]] shoots\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Add the [[Chicken|chicken]]  and [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients to a [[Lock and Lock box]], cover and shake really well to combine\n* Leave for a few hours to [[Marinade|marinade]], shaking now and then if you have the time\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Coat the rotary [[Air Fryer|air fryer]] with 1 tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Add the remaining [[Vegetable|vegetable]] mix ingredients into the [[Air-fryer|air-fryer]] pan and drizzle with the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| Cook on the highest temperature setting (usually for [[Chips|chips]]) for about 15 minutes\n| After the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] have cooked for about 10 minutes, leave them cooking while you add the [[Chicken|chicken]] [[Marinade|marinade]] to the [[Pro Breeze Air Fryer|pro breeze air fryer]] (the fan-[[Oven|oven]] type)\n| Cook for the marinaded chicken with the marinade for 10 minutes at 200\u00b0 C\n| By this time the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Onions|onions]] should have started to colour\n| Add the cooked [[Vegetables|vegetables]], [[Bean|bean]] shoots and [[Noodles|noodles]] to the [[Chicken|chicken]] mixture, stir well and cook for a further 5 minutes, stirring now and then\n| serve immediately\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Singapore_noodles_with_chicken_chicken_and_vegetables_with_noodles.jpg|Everything mixed together, ready to serve\nImage:Singapore_noodles_with_chicken_chicken_and_vegetables.jpg|The vegetables mixed in with the spicy chicken pieces\nImage:Singapore_noodles_with_chicken_marinading.jpg|The chicken after a few hours in the Tefal air-fryer\nImage:Singapore_noodles_with_chicken_colourful_ingredients.jpg|Most of the very colourful ingredients\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nA few quartered [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] were a nice fresh [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to this dish\n===Variations===\nAny chopped [[Vegetables|vegetables]] work well in this, especially, oddly, [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]]!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli                         "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Apem cake (translation), Indian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cake #flour #coconutmilk #yeast #riceflour #dough #pancake #snack #knead #rest #savory \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This 'street food' recipe was added by an Indonesian visitor: ROWI\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 5214\n|PortionCalories = 521\n|DatePublished=22nd May 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Klappertaart\n|Servings = Serves 10\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 55 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 40 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Coconut custard klappertaart-wiki.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Thanks Rowi</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It's lovely to get authentic recipes from our visitors!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n==Editor's notes==\nThis 'street food' recipe was added by an Indonesian visitor: [[User:ROWI]]. It was added in the Indonesian language so for the benefit of others, I have translated the recipe from Indonesian using Google Translate and formatted it for [[Cookipedia]]'s recipe pages.\n\nWe do not have an Indonesian or Javanese category so I have added it to the closest geographical categories we have to Indonesia: Chinese and Indian.\n\nThe original recipe and related references can be found in the ''See also'' section.\n\n[[User:Chef|Jerry, aka Chef]] ([[User talk:Chef|talk]])\n\n\n\nMake cooking or food is an exciting hobby. Not only for women but also for men and even children and adolescents. A variety of menus ranging [[Snacks|snacks]] to heavy meals can be prepared and processed foods dikreasi be new and unique. Traditional and unique and still remain stable even still be an idol. It is true what people say that \"taste never lie\", as evidenced by the good food will still taste delicious on the [[Tongue|tongue]] yet. Well on this one website to review many typical Indonesian food menu. Variety can be known to her directly by visiting the site directly. For example, here is one menu that has been presented, namely apem [[Cake|cake]]. There are not yet familiar with apem [[Cake|cake]]? If Java people would know yes. Apem national language is [[Pancakes|pancakes]], and international language is its dorayaki cake Doraemon (Japan has) he he he. Whatever its name, the same shape, so yes it doang. Most modified slightly contrived nothing like wings wide, there are built like a flying saucer aircraft, there is a simple round doang sprawl, all sorts lah. Well we all know yet what makes this delicious [[Pancake|pancake]] until hunted many culinary connoisseur? Nothing less than the tender [[Meat|meat]] chewy, sweet and distinctive taste like [[Coconut|coconut]] sticky [[Savory|savory]] mixes, and unique texture when cut open his flesh like a pattern perforated like a honeycomb.\n\nSERABINYA JAVA-[[Cake|cake]] APEM In the Java community, this [[Cake|cake]] easily found in traditional markets, [[Vegetable|vegetable]] stalls, night market, and even being sold by street vendors on the roadside. In addition as a [[Snack|snack]], this cake usually served at a celebration event in Java or known by the name \"berkahan\". Sometimes on the show \"ruwahan\" or \"nyadran\" ada.-Nyadran is also clean-up activities tomb area, usually performed in conjunction with the fasting month-.\n\nAPEM-easy or hard MAKE IT? The [[Cake|cake]] is quite unique [[Snack|snack]]. One that makes it unique is the way to cook it. In the Java community, there apem cooking that uses a special mold made of clay, but many also have used common molds that are sold freely in the market or supermarket. Cook it must also be careful not to use too large a [[Stove|stove]] fire. A small flame that is important enough heat evenly. Here's a little review about the ins and outs of how to make a [[Cake|cake]] apem with the materials needed as well as other important things. Nothing is hidden or secret recipe. Indonesian recipes kitchen team will review it briefly but clearly is solid and has been successfully tried and succeeded.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 250 g [[Rice flour|rice flour]]\n| 200 g [[Flour|flour]]\n| 2 tablespoons instant [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 200 g [[Fermented|fermented]] [[Cassava|cassava]] which has been crushed\n| 200 g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 2 [[free range eggs]]\n| 500 ml of warm [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]]\n| half teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Vanilla|vanilla]] powder\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Material source: mix [[Yeast|yeast]] with 2 tablespoons [[Flour|flour]], [[Knead|knead]] with a little added water until smooth. And diamlan for about 15 minutes\n| Combine the [[Rest|rest]] of the [[Flour|flour]] with [[Rice flour|rice flour]], [[Sugar|sugar]], sticky tape, and [[Salt|salt]]. Mix well and add the source material. [[Knead]] the [[Dough|dough]], adding the [[Egg|egg]] and warm [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]] little by little. Continue to knead until the dough becomes smooth. After that, allow the dough for 1 hour.\n| [[Dough]] will inflate after 1 hour settling. Then stir evenly. 4. Preheat apem cookie cutters, and do not forget to spread with [[Oil|oil]]. Pour [[Batter|batter]] into each mold, each one spoon, then closed. Cook for 5 minutes.\n|Behind the dough with the help of a spoon, then continue to cook again until done.\n|Remove and serve while warm.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nApem more delicious when eaten while warm, flesh firmness when it's cold turned into a bit stiff / hard.\n===Variations===\nThat was the basis of [[Cake|cake]] recipes apem / [[Pancake|pancake]]. Let me look different, you can add sprinkles meses creation with [[Chocolate|chocolate]] or [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]] on top as well. Or might want to try was given pieces of [[Pineapple|pineapple]], [[Strawberry|strawberry]], or jackfruit on it also allowed. Good luck and enjoy the delights apem.\n==See also==\n* [[User:ROWI|Recipe (in Indonesian) as added by User:ROWI]]\n* [http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Klappertaart Coconut cake 'Klappertarrt' - Wikipedia]\n* [http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kue Indonesian snacks 'Kue' - Wikipedia]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cake #flour #coconutmilk #yeast #riceflour #dough #pancake #snack #knead #rest #savory </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Aromatic cod in tomato sauce Chinese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fish #grill #chillipowder #cod #sauce #aromaticcodintomatosauce #cinnamon #mashedpotatoes #groundnutoil #tomatopuree #sesameoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A highly spiced Chinese-style recipe that goes brilliantly with mashed potatoes. For recipe that calls for cod, we always use basa\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 820\n|PortionCalories = 205\n|DatePublished=24th June 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chinese aromatic cod in tomato sauce recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Best with Basa.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Make spicy Friday fish-cakes, for a change, make them like this and you'll like them!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Use a Lock and Lock box to coat the fillets.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Use a Lock and Lock box to coat the fillets]]\n\nA highly spiced [[Chinese]]-style recipe that goes brilliantly with [[Mashed potatoes|mashed potatoes]].\n\nAs with any recipe that calls for [[Cod|cod]], we always use [[Basa fillets|basa fillets]] as I think they are tastier and also sustainable.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 4 [[Cod|cod]] fillets, or nicer still, 4 [[Basa fillets|basa fillets]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n}}\n'''dry rub'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 tablespoons [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Garlic powder|garlic powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ginger powder|ginger powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Fennel seeds|fennel seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] to a powder\n}}\n'''[[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Garam masala|garam masala]] powder\n| 1 teaspoon [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Ginger root|ginger root]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]]\n| &#189; teaspoon fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| 175 ml water\n| 1 tablespoon [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]]\n| 4 [[Szechuan peppercorns|szechuan peppercorns]]\n| 4 [[Black peppercorns|black peppercorns]]\n| 1 fresh [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| A very small piece of [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| Freshly chopped [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Grill|grill]] to high\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| MIx the dry rub ingredients together and place in a [[Lock and Lock box]] with the [[Fish|fish]] fillets, close the lid and shake gently to coat the [[Fish|fish]] evenly\n| Once the [[Grill|grill]] is nice and hot, reduce the heat to about half and lightly [[Spray|spray]] a [[Griddle pan|griddle pan]] with [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]] to prevent the fillets from sticking\n| [[Grill]] the fillets for 5 minutes on one side and then spoon the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]] over the fillets.  Turn and [[Grill|grill]] for 5 minutes on the other side\n| Check the [[Fish|fish]] is properly cooked, set to one side and keep warm\n| Make the [[Sauce|sauce]] by mixing the [[Garam masala|garam masala]], [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]], [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]] and water. Ensure the ingredients are well mixed\n| Heat the [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]] and add the whole [[Peppercorns|peppercorns]], [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] and [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]].  [[Stir fry]] for a minute or so\n| Reduce the heat and carefully add the [[Sauce|sauce]] mixture\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], reduce and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 5 minutes\n| Gently add the [[Fish|fish]] pieces to the [[Sauce|sauce]] and [[Poach|poach]] for a few minutes\n| Remove the cinnamon stick and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Mashed potatoes|mashed potatoes]], and garnish with chopped [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]]\n===Variations===\nUse [[Cod|cod]], [[Basa|basa]], or any firm fleshed [[Fish|fish]].  [[Tuna]] would be good too.\n===Chef's notes===\nUse a mild(ish) [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] or reduce the quantities as this might be too hot otherwise.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #grill #chillipowder #cod #sauce #aromaticcodintomatosauce #cinnamon #mashedpotatoes #groundnutoil #tomatopuree #sesameoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Baked sea bass (Chinese style)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked sea bass (Chinese style) a Chinese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fish #blackbeans #springonions #darksoysauce #wine #trout #anchovies #onion #seabass #baking #specialfriedrice \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a quick, fresh tasting dish that works brilliantly with sea bass, but most large white-fleshed fish would be just as good\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1118\n|PortionCalories = 279\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |ImageComment = Ready to serve, excuse the test 'hole'!\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Sea bass in ginger-done.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love sea bass</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Expensive, but worth every penny</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Sea bass in ginger.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Rubbed with sea salt, black pepper and ginger powder]]\nThis is a quick, fresh tasting dish that works brilliantly with [[sea bass]], but most large [[white-fleshed fish]] would be just as good. Carp would be fine if you can get it.\n\nThe time I cooked and photographed this meal I could not get [[spring onions]] or [[black beans]] so I used a small [[onion]], sliced thinly and 4 large [[anchovies]], finely chopped, instead of the [[black beans]].  I also used two small sea bass instead of 1 large.  Moral: Don't go shopping late on a Bank Holiday Sunday! However, it was still a great success.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1  750g (1.5 lbs) whole [[fish]], [[sea bass]], [[trout]] or carp, cleaned and gutted (use two if you can only get small fish)\n| 1 teaspoon [[sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[ground ginger powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon salted [[black beans]], soaked, drained and crushed lightly, or 4 large [[anchovies]], finely chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[dark soy sauce]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[sugar]]\n| 1 tablespoon Chinese [[wine]] or [[dry sherry]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[root ginger]], peeled and finely [[shredded]]\n| 2 star anise, broken into small pieces\n| 2 [[spring onions]], [[cut on the diagonal]], or 1 small [[onion]], peeled and finely sliced\n| 2 tablespoons [[vegetable oil]]\n| Sheet of [[tin foil]], large enough to wrap loosely around the [[fish]]\n| '''Dressing'''\n| 1tbs [[light soy sauce]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[sesame oil]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Descale]], rinse and and dry the [[fish]]\n| With a sharp knife make deep cuts across both sides of the [[fish]].  On a very large fish make criss-cross cuts\n| Mix the [[salt]], [[pepper]] and [[ginger powder]] together and rub well into the slashes in the [[fish]]\n| Mix the crushed [[black beans]], [[dark soy sauce]], [[sugar]] and Chinese [[wine]]\n| Sprinkle the shredded ginger and [[spring onions]] on the tin foil and lay the [[fish]] on top\n| Heat 2 tablespoons of [[oil]] until [[smoking]] and carefully pour this all over the [[fish]]\n| When the [[oil]] has cooled a little, spread the [[black bean]] mixture all over the [[fish]] and in the cavity\n| Arrange the broken star anise pieces throughout the cavity of the fish\n| Bring the foil up and seal well and place on a [[baking]] tray\n| [[bake]] for 20 minutes or until the [[fish]] is tender\n| Arrange on a serving platter and pour the [[soy]] dressing over the [[fish]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe immediately.\n\nThis is nice with [[special fried rice]] and a [[green salad]]\n===Chef's tip===\nIf you use two small fish instead of 1 large, as long as your tin foil is large enough, it's probably better to use 1 foil parcel for both fish as the flavours seem to mingle better. \n===Variation===\nThis recipe would work equally well with [[trout]].\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #blackbeans #springonions #darksoysauce #wine #trout #anchovies #onion #seabass #baking #specialfriedrice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Bang, bang chicken, a noisy Chinese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #bangbangsauce #cucumber #onion #bangbangchicken #garlic #bouquetgarni #unusualrecipes #tea #sauce #chickenstock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Bang-bang chicken is a deliciously spicy Chinese dish that is easier to make than it first might seem\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 813\n|PortionCalories = 203\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = It doesn't look brilliant on the plate, but it was gorgeous & is going on my repertoire!\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Bang bang chicken recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely sauce</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Perfect with chicken</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Bang bang sauce.jpg|thumb|300px|right|[[Bang bang sauce]]]]\nBang-bang [[Chicken|chicken]] is a deliciously spicy Chinese dish that is easier to make than it first might seem.\n\nIf you're wondering, bang!, bang! is the noise of the [[wooden mallet]], traditionally used to [[flatten the cooked chicken]] to make it easier to shred.\n\n'''for the chicken'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 skinless, boneless [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts, about 450 g (1 lb) in total weight\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| &frac12; teaspoon whole [[Black peppercorns|black peppercorns]]\n| 1 small unpeeled [[Onion|onion]], halved\n| 1 [[bouquet garni]] - optional\n}}\n'''for the garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 large [[Cucumber|cucumber]], peeled, de-seeded and cut into thin strips. If, like me, you are a lazy cook, slice it in a [[Food processor|food processor]]!\n| 1 serving of [[bang bang sauce]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Chili oil recipe (quick)|quick chili oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Chicken|chicken]] in a small saucepan and just cover with water\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Peppercorns|peppercorns]] the [[Onion|onion]] and optionally, the [[bouquet garni]].\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], skim off any scum. Cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 20-25 minutes\n| Remove the [[Chicken|chicken]] and pat dry with a clean [[Tea|tea]]-towel\n| (If making bang bang [[Sauce|sauce]], use 3 tablespoons of the cooking liquid to thin the [[Tahini|tahini]])\n| Freeze the remaining liquid as [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Smash the [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts flat with a rolling-pin or the (clean) base of a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]]. Bang! Bang!\n| Shred the [[Chicken|chicken]] with two forks\n| Arrange the [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Cucumber|cucumber]] on a serving dish and drizzle with [[bang bang sauce]] and [[Chili oil|chili oil]]\n}}\n===Variations===\nI love the combination of spring onions and cucumber, so, although not authentic, I like to add chopped spring onions to this dish, about 6 to go with 1 whole cucumber.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #bangbangsauce #cucumber #onion #bangbangchicken #garlic #bouquetgarni #unusualrecipes #tea #sauce #chickenstock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Beef Massaman curry (slow cooker recipe)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Thai Beef Massaman curry (slow cooker recipe)\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#wok #coconutmilk #grated #thai #vegetablestock #beefstock #nampla #slowcooker #newpotatoes #coriander #juice \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Beef Massaman curry (Thai: \u0e41\u0e01\u0e07\u0e21\u0e31\u0e2a\u0e21\u0e31\u0e48\u0e19, is a rich, relatively mild Thai curry that is an interpretation of a Persian dish\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 6047\n|PortionCalories = 1511\n|DatePublished=2nd November 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Served with brown rice and green beans - not coriander so parsley will have to do! \n|Servings = 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  8 hours, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  8 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Beef Massaman curry slow cooker recipe recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Almost like a vindaloo</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..without the heat.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Beef Massaman curry]] ([[Thai]]: &#3649;&#3585;&#3591;&#3617;&#3633;&#3626;&#3617;&#3633;&#3656;&#3609;, RTGS: [[Kaeng matsaman|kaeng matsaman]], IPA: [k&#603;&#720;&#331; m\u00e1t.sa.m\u00e0n]) is a rich, relatively mild Thai [[Curry|curry]] that is an interpretation of a Persian dish.\n\nMassaman or matsaman is not a native [[Thai]] word. It is generally thought to refer to the Muslims with earlier writers from the mid-19th century calling the dish \"[[Mussulman curry]]\"; Mussulman being an archaic form of the word Muslim.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 500g/1lb 2oz [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 800g (1lb 12oz) beef shin, cut into bite-sized pieces\n| 3 tablespoons [[Massaman curry|massaman curry]] paste\n| 5cm (2\") fresh [[Root ginger|root ginger]], peeled and [[Grated|grated]]\n| Bunch fresh [[Coriander|coriander]], stalks separated and finely chopped\n| 400ml (14fl oz) tin [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| [[Grated]] [[Zest|zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| [[Grated]] [[Zest|zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[lemon]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Nam pla|nam pla]] ([[Fish sauce|fish sauce]])\n| 150 ml [[Beef stock]] or [[vegetable stock]] as needed\n}}\n'''garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| A handful of roughly chopped [[Roasted|roasted]] unsalted [[Peanuts|peanuts]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Halve the [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]] and pop them in the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]]\n| Heat a [[Wok|wok]] or [[Frying pan|frying pan]], add the [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Oil|oil]] and [[Brown|brown]] the [[Meat|meat]] in small batches\n| Add the [[Meat|meat]] to the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]] as each batch is [[Browned|browned]]\n| Next add the massaman paste, [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Coriander|coriander]] stalks to the [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a few minutes\n| Add the [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]] to the [[Wok|wok]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Reduce the heat, mix in the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Lime zest|lime zest]] and [[Nam pla|nam pla]] and pour this mixture over the [[Meat|meat]] and [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| Add enough [[beef stock]] or [[vegetable stock]] to cover the meat and potatoes, rinsing out the [[coconut milk]] can with it first. \n| Stir well, pop the lid on and slow cook on low for 8 hours\n| After 8 hours, ladle off any excess [[Fat|fat]] and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with [[Lime wedges|lime wedges]], chopped [[Peanuts|peanuts]] and [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]].  Serve with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]].\n===Variations===\n'''Turn it fruity:''' I chopped up a few [[pineapple]] rings, left over from making [[Chicken satay]] and added at the start of the cooking stage and also a little pineapple juice together with a handful of raisins.  Finally I added a chopped up [[banana]] but only at the very end of the cooking process, just long enough for them to warm up.  This is probably not authentic, but it's nice to have a sweet curry now and then! \n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Thai recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#wok #coconutmilk #grated #thai #vegetablestock #beefstock #nampla #slowcooker #newpotatoes #coriander #juice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

cup stock, [[soy sauce]], [[sugar]], and [[sesame oil]], and stir until [[sugar]] dissolves\n| In a third small bowl, dissolve [[cornflour]] in [[wine]] or [[sherry]]\n| Just before serving, heat a wok over high heat\n| Add [[ghee]] and heat until almost smoking\n| [[Frying|Fry]] the [[onion]] and [[red pepper]] for a minute then add [[Garlic|garlic]] and bean mixture and cook for 15 seconds, or until fragrant but not brown\n| Add [[seafood]] and [[stir-fry]] for 1 minute\n| Add stock-based sauce and cook for 2 to 5 minutes, or until seafood is cooked; if necessary to prevent mixture from sticking to pan, add remaining stock\n| Stir [[cornflour]] mixture and add to [[stir-fry]] along with green [[spring onion]] parts and sliced vegetables\n| Bring sauce to a boil\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe immediately with [[Boiled rice|plain boiled rice]].\n===Variations===\nReplace seafood with [[pork fillet]] or [[chicken]]\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #cornflour #blackbeanprawnstirfry #sesameoil #springonions #chillies #onion #sherry #ghee #seafood #frying </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Cajun Chicken Stir Fry",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Cajun Chicken Noodle Stir Fry\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #oliveoil #tastesensationcajunseasoning #vegetables #stirfry #chickenbreast #poultryrecipes #noodles #vegetablerecipes #chineserecipes #northamericanrecipes\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=Another experiment with Taste Sensation taste sensation seasonings. Cajun Chicken Noodle Stir Fry That sounds weird!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=18th December 2019\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  3 hours, 17 minutes\n|PrepTime =  3 hours, 5 minutes\n|CookTime =  12 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 467\n|PortionCalories = 23\n|Image = [[Image:Cajun Chicken Stir Fry recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">This was good - I remember making it</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And I can taste it from the photograph!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning chicken pieces, air-fried.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After 10 minutes in the air fryer basket]]\n[[Image:Cajun Seasoning, Lime Juice, Olive oil mixed.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After shaking the sealed box for 10 seconds]]\n[[Image:Cajun Seasoning, Lime Juice, Olive oil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning, olive oil and lime juice]]\nAnother experiment with [[Taste Sensation Seasonings]].\nCajun Chicken Noodle Stir Fry! That sounds weird, but I bet it will be fine.  I marinaded the chicken slices in lime juice for an hour, then added the Cajun Seasoning and a tablespoon of olive oil to a Lock and Lock box, closed the lid and shook for ten seconds.  This leaves the chicken perfectly coated.  It could be stir fried on a wok but I'm going to air fry it in the basket so it can be cooked with no extra oil.\n\nI've used the remains of the Morrisons pre-packed [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] ingredients from yesterday's [[Chilli and lime chicken stir fry]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 large [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]], cut into thin strips\n| 2 tablespoons of [[lime juice]]\n| 1 heaped tablespoon of [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]]\n| 3 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Half a packet of [[Bean sprouts|bean sprouts]] [180 g]\n| Half a packet of fresh [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]] [205 g]\n| Half a packet of Sweet & Crunchy [[Stir fry|stir fry]] [300 g]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you get the chance, marinade the chicken pieces in lime juice for an hour before you add the Cajun Seasoning\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop the sliced [[Chicken|chicken]] in a [[Lock and Lock box|lock and lock box]] together with the [[Taste Sensation Cajun Seasoning]] and one of the tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].  Shake like crazy to mix.  Leave to [[Marinade|marinade]] for a while longer if you can.\n| This is quicker and easier if you have two woks, if not cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] first and keep warm while you cook the [[Vegetables|vegetables]]\n| [[Stir fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], turning regularly until the chicken is properly cooked - about 5 minutes or longer if it's thickly sliced\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until they are wilted\n| Toss in the [[Beans|beans]] shoots and [[Noodles|noodles]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] until cooked - about 4 minutes\n| Mix in the cooked [[Chicken|chicken]] and serve immediately\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can also cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] in an air-fryer basket for about 5 minutes, instead of pan-[[Frying|frying]]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#chicken #oliveoil #tastesensationcajunseasoning #vegetables #stirfry #chickenbreast #poultryrecipes #noodles #vegetablerecipes #chineserecipes #northamericanrecipes</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It is generally thought to refer to the Muslims with earlier writers from the mid-19th century calling the dish \"Mussulman [[Curry|curry]]\"; Mussulman being an archaic form of the word Muslim.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 450 g (1 lb) of boneless [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]] cut into bite-sized pieces\n| 500g/1lb 2oz of [[Potatoes|boiling potatoes]], cut into matchbox sized pieces\n| 2 tablespoons [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and sliced\n| 5 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 5 cm (2\") [[Fresh ginger|fresh ginger]], peeled and roughly [[Grated|grated]]\n| 2 [[Red chillies|red chillies]], sliced, or to taste\n| 142 ml (\u00bc pint) of good strong [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 1 stalk [[Lemongrass|lemongrass]], chopped and bashed in a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]], or 3 tablespoons of prepared lemongrass\n| 5 [[Kaffir lime leaves|kaffir lime leaves]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Turmeric powder|turmeric powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]] [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground|ground]] white [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| [[Seeds]] from 2 [[Black cardamom pods|black cardamom pods]], freshly [[Ground|ground]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Tamarind paste|tamarind paste]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Nam pla|nam pla]] ([[Fish sauce|fish sauce]])\n| 1 teaspoon [[Shrimp paste|shrimp paste]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| 1 small [[Red pepper|red pepper]], de-seeded and thinly sliced\n| 1 large fresh [[tomato]], peeled if you wish, and chopped\n}}\n'''garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Roasted]] unsalted [[Cashew nuts|cashew nuts]] or [[Peanuts|peanuts]], chopped\n| [[Coriander leaves]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you have the time, [[Marinade|marinade]] the [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]] in a little [[Lemon|lemon]] or [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and a large pinch of [[Salt|salt]] for a few hours a cool place.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]] to a [[Wok|wok]] and [[Saute|saute]] the [[Onions|onions]].  Once they are lightly [[Browned|browned]], [[Stir fry|stir fry]] the [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] for a minute or so.  Don't allow the garlic to burn.\n| Add [[Kaffir lime leaves|kaffir lime leaves]], [[Lemongrass|lemongrass]], [[Turmeric|turmeric]], [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]], [[Ground cumin seeds|ground cumin seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] [[Cardamom|cardamom]], [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] [[Seeds|seeds]], [[Black pepper|black pepper]],  [[Tamarind paste|tamarind paste]], [[Nam pla|nam pla]], [[Shrimp paste|shrimp paste]] and [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]].\n| Mix this well to combine and add the [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]].\n| Add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces, bring to a [[Boil|boil]] then reduce the heat, cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 40 minutes or until the potatoes are cooked.\n| Pop the chopped tomato and red pepper into the curry when there is 15 minutes to go.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a little [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]], remembering that you already have [[Potatoes|potatoes]] in this dish.\n\nGarnish with chopped [[Nuts|nuts]] and [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]].\n===Variations===\nIf you don;t have [[Kaffir lime leaves|kaffir lime leaves]], use 2 [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], fresh or [[Dried|dried]].  The flavour won;t be the same but the [[Bay|bay]] leaves do add a little more flavour\n===Chef's notes===\nFor extra flavour, chop the stalks from the [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] and add them to the [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] while you are bashing the [[Lemongrass|lemongrass]].\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Thai recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenmassamancurry #ground #corianderleaves #seeds #kaffirlimeleaves #lemongrass #jaggery #tamarindpaste #massamancurry #brownsugar #curry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chicken satay",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken satay recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #chickensatay #chickenthighs #sataysauce #corianderleaves #springonions #ginger #marinade #peanutbutter #cuminseeds #pineapple \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is my version of Jamie Oliver's Chicken satay his recent book, Jamie Oliver's Comfort Food\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1892\n|PortionCalories = 473\n|DatePublished=4th November 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  12 hours, 40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  12 hours, 20 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken satay recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Thanks Jamie!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Brilliant.  I love this!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nThis is my version of Jamie Oliver's [[Chicken]] [[Satay]] from '''Jamie Oliver's Comfort Food''' ''August 2014'', ISBN 978-071815953\n\nI've really just changed some of the ingredients and omitted the unsalted shelled [[Peanuts|peanuts]] as the garnish as Anne does not like peanuts.  She loves [[Satay sauce|satay sauce]] though.  Odd, I know!\n\nAs with any [[Chicken|chicken]] dish, I [[Marinade|marinade]] the chicken pieces in a few tablespoons of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], half a teaspoon of fine [[Salt|salt]] and a splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].  This was a useful tip picked up on my first [[Indian cookery]] class, many moons ago.  I've also added a dash of [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]]. My [[Jaccard meat tenderiser]] has been brought into play on chicken for the first time.  We'll see if that makes any noticeable difference.\n\nI've used bone in [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]] as they were inexpensive.  These are not idea for skewering so I'll cook them in the [[Oven|oven]] and eat around the [[bones]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 8 [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon fine [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]]\n| 1 teaspoon medium [[Curry powder|curry powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Turmeric powder|turmeric powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon sugar\n| \u00bd teaspoon white [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| \u00bd teaspoon [[Black cumin seeds|black cumin seeds]]\n| 2 [[Green Indian chillies|green indian chillies]]\n| 2 [[Red chillies|red chillies]]\n| 4 [[Fat|fat]] [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| Thumb-sized piece of [[Ginger|ginger]], peeled and roughly chopped\n| Bunch of [[Spring onions|spring onions]]\n| Bunch of fresh [[Coriander|coriander]]\n| 6 tablespoons crunchy [[Peanut butter|peanut butter]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Tahini|tahini]]\n| 3 [[Limes|limes]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Light soy sauce|light soy sauce]]\n| [[Peanut oil]]\n| Small tin of [[Pineapple|pineapple]] rings\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Remove the skin from the [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]].  If you're lucky enough to own a [[Jaccard meat tenderiser]], press lots of holes into the [[Chicken|chicken]].  Add the chicken pieces  and [[Marinade|marinade]] for 6 hours of so in a cool place.\n* A few hours before you want to cook the [[Chicken|chicken]], cut some big slashes in them so there are large surface areas for the cover. Pop them in a [[Lock and Lock box]] with the half of the [[Satay sauce|satay sauce]]. Shake well and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for a few hours.\n* 30 minutes before you're ready to cook, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] and a [[Griddle pan|griddle pan]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| De-seed one of each of the [[green chillies]] and one of the [[Red chillies|red chillies]] and peel and roughly chop the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[ginger]].\n| In a dry pan, heat the [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] until they pop.  Grind them in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]] or [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]], pop them back into the pan with the [[Curry powder|curry powder]] and [[Turmeric|turmeric]] for 30 seconds to release the aromas.\n| Reserve a handful of [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] for garnish and pop the [[Rest|rest]] in a [[Blender|blender]] together with two chopped [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Blend|blend]] to a paste.\n| Add the [[Peanut butter|peanut butter]] and [[Tahini|tahini]], [[Zest|zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 2 [[Limes|limes]], 2 tablespoons of [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]], 1 teaspoon of sugar and the green parts of the [[Spring onions|spring onions]].\n| Blend and test for seasoning. Adjust the consistency by adding a little [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] or water if needed.\n| Reserve half of the [[Satay sauce|satay sauce]] to serve as a garnish, cut a few slashes in the [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]], pop them in a [[Lock and Lock box]] with the remaining [[Sauce|sauce]] and [[Marinade|marinade]] in a cool place for a few hours.\n| [[Spray]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces with a little [[Oil|oil]], carefully oil the hot [[Griddle pan|griddle pan]] and cook in the [[Oven|oven]] for 20 minutes, turning after 10 minutes.\n| Chop the remaining [[Chillies|chillies]], the white parts of the [[Spring onions|spring onions]] and the [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] to use as a garnish.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken satay conventional.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Served in a more conventional manner, with a vegetable stir-fry and noodles ([[vegetable chow mein]])\nImage:Chicken satay sspread.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Really should have been with paratha or naan breads but pittas worked pretty well\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the remaining [[Satay sauce|satay sauce]], [[Lime wedges|lime wedges]], [[pineapple]] rings, [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] and [[Pitta breads|pitta breads]] or more conventionally with [[vegetable chow-mein]] (stir fried vegetables and noodles).\n===Variations===\nUse boneless [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]], chop them into 4 before [[Marinating|marinating]] and cook them on [[Skewers|skewers]]\n===Chef's notes===\nBe aware of food hygiene when preparing this dish as you will be handling raw [[Chicken|chicken]] multiple times and preparing items that will be [[Uncooked|uncooked]] and used as garnishes.\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Mauritian recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental I used their excellent [[Chilli and Lime Seasoning]] recently in [[Chili and lime spiced butternut squash]].  This time I thought I would try a [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]].\n\nI've used Morrisons pre-packed [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] ingredients as they are the easiest way to get a decent variety of [[Vegetables|vegetables]].  Half quantities of these packs are perfect for a two-person [[Stir fry|stir fry]].  Just check the quality of the [[Bean sprouts|bean sprouts]] as they can be rather close to sell-by (or bin-by) [[Date|date]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 large [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]], cut into thin strips\n| 1 heaped tablespoon of [[Taste Sensation Chilli and Lime Seasoning]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Half a packet of [[Bean sprouts|bean sprouts]] [180 g]\n| Half a packet of fresh [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]] [205 g]\n| Half a packet of Sweet & Crunchy [[Stir fry|stir fry]] [300 g]\n| Splash of [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]] - optional\n| Splash of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]] - optional\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you get the chance, leave the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces, dusted with the [[Taste Sensation Chilli and Lime Seasoning]] in the [[refrigerator]] for a few hours beforehand to enhance the flavour.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop the sliced [[Chicken|chicken]] in a [[Lock and Lock box|lock and lock box]] together with the [[Taste Sensation Chilli and Lime Seasoning]] and one of the tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].  Shake like crazy to mix.  Leave to [[Marinade|marinade]] for a while if you get the chance.\n| This is quicker and easier if you have two woks, if not cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] first and keep warm while you cook the [[Vegetables|vegetables]]\n| [[Stir fry]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], turning regularly until the chicken is properly cooked - about 5 minutes or longer if it's thickly sliced\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until they are wilted\n| Toss in the [[Beans|beans]] shoots and [[Noodles|noodles]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] until cooked - about 4 minutes\n| If using, add a splash of [[Sherry|sherry]] and [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]] and mix well\n| Mix in the cooked [[Chicken|chicken]] and serve immediately\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can also cook the [[Chicken|chicken]] in an air-fryer basket for about 5 minutes, instead of pan-[[Frying|frying]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #oliveoil #vegetables #stirfry #beansprouts #chilliandlimechickenstirfry #refrigerator #noodles #drysherry #tastesensationrecipes #date </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

440 ml tin of [[Beer|beer]] of your choice\n* [[Sesame oil]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - Gas 6)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove any A small chicken sits quite happily; a large chicken might be a bit trickier\n# Place the [[Baking tray|baking tray]] in the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]]\n# After 30 minutes, reduce the heat to 180\u00b0 C ( 350\u00b0 F - Gas 4)\n# The [[Chicken|chicken]] should be cooked in about 1.5 hours, depending upon the size of the bird. Check every 15 minutes towards the end.  It is done when the juices run clear if the deepest part of the flesh (eg the thigh) is pierced with a metal skewer or sharp knife\n# Remove the [[Chicken|chicken]] extremely carefully with [[Oven gloves|oven gloves]] and tongs if needed.\n===Serving suggestions===\nAllow to [[Rest for|rest for]] 10 minutes before carving\n{{Template:Beercan chicken - See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #chinesebeercanchicken #beer #boiling #sesameoil #beercan #beercanchicken #restfor #marinade #brownsugar #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Granulated sugar|granulated sugar]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove the stalks from the [[Chillies|chillies]].\n| Slice in half, lengthways and remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] and any white pith.\n| Leave the [[Chillies|chillies]] soaking overnight in the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Vinegar|vinegar]].\n| Pulse to a pur\u00e9e in a [[Food processor|food processor]].\n| Add the [[garlic powder]], [[Cornflour|cornflour]] and [[Sugar|sugar]] and adjust the consistency to your liking with a little water.  Pulse to mix.\n| Pour into a [[Sterilised|sterilised]] bottle.\n| This will keep forever!\n}}\n===Servinghs===\nServings: 35 - Makes one 350 g (12 oz) bottle of [[chilli sauce]]\n===Variations===\nIf you don't have white Chinese [[Rice vinegar|rice vinegar]] you can use white distilled [[Malt vinegar|malt vinegar]].  You can also substitute [[arrowroot]] for the [[cornflour]].\n==See also==\n* [[Chilli sauce|Many other chilli sauce recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chinesechilliandgarlicsauce #chillies #cornflour #ricevinegar #garlicpowder #granulatedsugar #unusualrecipes #foodprocessor #maltvinegar #seeds #sterilised </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chinese style pickled cauliflower",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chinese style pickled cauliflower recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cauliflower #blackvinegar #chinesestylepickledcauliflower #pickle #saladspinner #vinegar #spices #teatowel #sterilise #seewoo #frozen \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An experimental recipe for pickled cauliflower using just Chinkiang black (rice) vinegar\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 125\n|PortionCalories = 11\n|DatePublished=12th May 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Servings: 12 - Makes almost a litre of pickled cauliflower\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 1 day\n|PrepTime = 1 day\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Chinese style pickled cauliflower recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Can't find Balck Vinegar?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2.55</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Tried everywhere and can't find anything like the price you paid.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:WorkInProgress}}\nWe were gifted an absolutely massive [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]] recently, most of which was [[Vacuum packed|vacuum packed]] and [[Frozen|frozen]] for later use.  I decided to make a [[Pickle|pickle]] with what was left.\n\nMost of the flavour of a [[Pickle|pickle]] is from the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] plus any additional [[Spices|spices]].  I absolutely love the flavour of Chinkiang [[Black vinegar|black vinegar]], it's so nice you could almost [[Drink|drink]] it.  As I want to retain the flavour of the Chinkiang black rice vinegar and not sully it with any other flavours, I'm using just the vinegar and the [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]].\n\nTo hold all of the pieces of [[cauliflower]] under the vinegar and prevent them from going mouldy, I used an odd piece of sterilised plastic to cover them.  If you are going to do this only use plastic as most metals will corrode in the vinegar.  Some commercial pickles actually come with a plastic disc that performs this function that you might be able to reuse.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 500 g of small [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]] florets trimmed from a cauliflower\n| 2 tablespoons fine [[Salt|salt]]\n| 3 550 ml bottles of Chinkiang [[Black vinegar|black vinegar]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]] florets to a bowl and just cover with cold water\n| Leave in a cool place for 24 hours.\n| RInse the florets in cold water and dry, ideally using a [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]]\n| Lay the florets out on a [[Tea towel|tea towel]], ideally in the sun or in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for a few hours\n| [[Sterilise]] a [[Kilner jar]], add the [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]] florets and cover with Chinkiang [[Black vinegar|black vinegar]]\n| Leave for 1 month to mature\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chinkiang black vinegar.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Chinkiang black vinegar (\u00a31.43 per 550ml [[See Woo]] May 2015)\nImage:Very large cauliflower.jpg|300px|thumb|right|A very large cauliflower!\n</gallery>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Pickles and preserves]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Pickled]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cauliflower #blackvinegar #chinesestylepickledcauliflower #pickle #saladspinner #vinegar #spices #teatowel #sterilise #seewoo #frozen </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

The original recipe contains aji-no-moto in place of the [[Lemon|lemon]].  This quirky [[Ingredient|ingredient]] can be found in some oriental food shops.  In this case you can substitute the lemon for 3 tsps aji-no-moto.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Sugar|sugar]] quantity seems rather large (as it does in many [[Spanish]] recipe books), so you may wish to start off with a smaller amount and then add more if desired.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lemon #thermomix #sauce #spanish #lemonjuice #vinegar #salads #chinese #ricevinegar #sesameoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I used half of a boneless aromatic crispy duck for the main topping\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2432\n|PortionCalories = 1216\n|DatePublished=2nd May 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Crispy duck and hoisin pizza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fab idea!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Don't think I've ever seen this before but it was really good.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAnother excuse to play with my [[homemade sous vide cooker]] and combine the results in a [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nI used half of a boneless aromatic [[Crispy duck|crispy duck]], bought from [[See Woo]], our brilliant local [[Chinese wholesalers]].  A couple of cooked [[Duck|duck]] breasts would work just as well on this [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\nI [[Vacuum packed|vacuum packed]] the half [[Duck|duck]] in 2 tablespoons of [[Peking duck|peking duck]] [[Sauce]] ([[Hoisin sauce]] is very similar) and cooked [[Sous vide|sous vide]] for 8 hours at 60\u00b0C and [[Shredded|shredded]] it ready for the [[Pizza topping|pizza topping]].  The duck would be perfectly cooked after 3 hours at 57\u00b0C, but I wanted to achieve the 'overcooked and falling apart' finish that you can't get with cooking for shorter times.  As it is vacuum sealed, it stays nice and moist and the quick heat from the grill give the duck a nice crispy finish.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 portion [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] - Makes 2 [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| 150g of selected [[Cheeses|cheeses]], [[Grated|grated]].\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza]]\n| 4 medium [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], sliced\n| 300 g  peking crispy [[Duck|duck]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| A large bunch of fresh [[Chives|chives]], chopped\n| [[Olive oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Grill|grill]] (if using a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]])\n* If using the [[Oven|oven]], preheat it to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Dust your work surface with [[Fine yellow cornmeal|fine yellow cornmeal]]\n| Divide the [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] into two and roll out into two thin 25.5 cm (10 inch) [[Pizzas|pizzas]]\n| You can leave them in a [[Warm place|warm place]] for an hour or so to rise. I quite like them cooked immediately they are rolled out for a more crispy finish.\n| Prick the [[Pizza|pizza]] all over with a fork. This prevents it puffing up too much and burning while it is cooking\n| With a deft move, slide the [[Pizza|pizza]] from the [[Pizza peel|pizza peel]], on to the preheated [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]].\n| Cook on one side only for about 2 minutes or until lightly [[Browned|browned]].\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and spread the [[Pizza|pizza]] with 2 tablespoons of [[Tomato sauce for pizza|tomato sauce for pizza]].\n| Sprinkle the cheese over the tomato sauce and top with the shredded duck.  Don't put the cheese on top of the duck if you want it to be crispy.\n| Season with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and finish with a drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is nicely melted. This should take about 4 minutes under a [[Grill|grill]] on a [[Pizza stone|pizza stone]], if oven [[Baking|baking]], about 15 minutes in the middle of the oven.\n| Repeat for the second [[Pizza|pizza]].\n| Keep the first [[Pizza|pizza]] warm at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] whilst you make the second.\n| Sprinkle with chopped chives and serve\n}}\n===See also===\n*[[Sous vide duck pizza]]\n*[[Sous vide hoisin duck pizza]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Pizza recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pizza #duck #pizzastone #crispyduckandhoisinpizza #grill #oliveoil #pizzas #pizzadough #shredded #bake #provolone </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Crispy duck pancakes recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Crispy duck pancakes, a Chinese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #frozen #sesameoil #flour #steam #pekingduck #crispyduck #pancakes #rollingpin #wok #crispyduckpancakesrecipe \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=You can buy crispy duck pancakes from any Asian wholesaler, usually frozen, or you can make your own using this recipe. Perfect for Peking duck\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1122\n|PortionCalories = 280\n|DatePublished=3rd August 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 -  Will make 18 [[pancakes]]\n|Difficulty = 1\n|ImageComment = Commercially made frozen Chinese pancakes\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 3 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 hour\n|CookTime = 3 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chinese pancakes.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Does anyone make this?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Really, you can buy these for a few pennies each - and freeze them, so why bother making them!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nYou can buy [[crispy duck pancakes]] from any [[:Category:Chinese ingredients (supplier)|Asian wholesaler]], usually [[frozen]], or you can make your own using this recipe.\n\nPerfect for [[Peking duck]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 275 g (10 oz) [[plain flour]] plus extra for dusting\n| 250 ml (8fl oz) water, just [[boiled]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[sesame oil]]\n| [[Flour]] for dusting\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large bowl, add all of the [[flour]] and gradually mix in the hot water, constantly mixing until all of the water has been added.\n| ''Tinker'': If the mixture is too dry, add a little bit more water; too wet, then a tiny bit more flour.\n| Tip the [[dough]] out onto a dusted work surface and hand knead it for almost 10 minutes. As with any [[dough]], tinker some more if needed.\n| Put the [[dough]] back in the bowl to rest for 30 minutes, covered with a damp cloth.\n| Back on to the work surface for another 5 minutes of kneading and tinkering.\n| When you have a smooth, pliable [[dough]], hand-roll into a sausage 45 cm (18\") long and 2.5cm(1\") thick.\n| Chop into 18 equal pieces and mould them into balls. Take two of the balls. Dip one side of one ball into the [[sesame oil]] and put the oiled side on top of the other ball.\n| Mass production! With a [[rolling pin]], roll the 2 pancakes simultaneously into a 15 cm (6\") disc. \n| Put the double pancake into a [[frying]]-pan or [[wok]] on a very gentle heat for a few minutes, really just to dry it out a little.\n| Turn it over and repeat for the other side.\n| Allow to cool, but before it gets cold, peel the two pancakes apart.\n| Do this with the remaining pairs of pancakes.\n| These can be [[frozen]] for later use.\n| [[Steam]] or microwave them to reheat and then serve with [[crispy duck]].\n}}\n==See also==\n* [[Traditional English pancakes]]\n* [[Breton buckwheat pancake recipe]]\n* [[Cr\u00eape recipe]]\n* [[Potato pancakes]]\n* [[Crispy duck pancake recipe]]\n* [[Crispy potato pancakes]]\n* '''Procedure to make a [[How to make crispy aromatic duck at home|complete crispy duck meal at home]].'''\n\n{{CategoryLine}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Steamed]]\n[[Category:Microwaved]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #frozen #sesameoil #flour #steam #pekingduck #crispyduck #pancakes #rollingpin #wok #crispyduckpancakesrecipe </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

one of may favourite dishes, and healthier this way. \ud83e\udd6c\ud83e\udd6c\ud83e\udd6c</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA healthy, [[Abel & Cole]] twist to the classic [[Chinese]] [[Crispy duck pancakes|crispy duck pancakes]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 2 [[Duck|duck]] legs\n| 1 [[Red chilli|red chilli]], chopped\n| 10 g [[Fresh ginger|fresh ginger]], chopped or [[Grated|grated]]\n| A splash of [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]]\n| 20 g drizzle of [[Honey|honey]]\n| 100 g [[Spring onions|spring onions]]\n| 1 300 g  [[Cucumber|cucumber]]\n| 8 large [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves\n| 50 ml [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| Fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] (optional)\n| Fresh [[Lime|lime]] (optional)\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Heat the [[Oven|oven]] to 160\u00b0 C (325\u00b0 F - gas 3), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 140\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop [[Duck|duck]] in a [[Roasting dish|roasting dish]]. Add [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]] and [[Honey|honey]]. Massage into [[Duck|duck]].\n| [[Roast]] for 45 mins. Then, crank the [[Oven|oven]] up to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] to [[Help|help]] crisp the skin; cook for 15 mins, till [[Duck|duck]] is crisp, golden and cooked through - test by piercing a [[Fat|fat]] part of the leg - if the juices run clear, it's done.\n| [[Rest for]] 15 mins.\n| Slice [[Onions|onions]] and [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] into wispy wands. Wash your [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves.\n| Shred the cooled [[Duck|duck]]. Spoon some [[Sauce|sauce]] over it. Fold through.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTo eat: [[Pile|pile]] a mound of saucy [[Duck|duck]] onto a leaf. Top with [[Cucumber|cucumber]] and [[Spring onion|spring onion]]. Add extra [[Sauce|sauce]], [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Lime|lime]], if you like.\n===Variations===\n[[Vegan]] option: Swap the [[Duck|duck]] for [[Brown rice|brown rice]] [[Noodles|noodles]]. Toss warm, cooked [[Noodles|noodles]] with a glug of [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]. [[Pile]] into leaves with garnishes, as above.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#duck #noodles #pile #hoisinsauce #lime #crispyduckparcels #sauce #lettuce #honey #cucumber #soysauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This is an ideal example of a way to use up your glut of cucumbers.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 450 g [1 lb] [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]]\n| 2 teaspoons fine [[Salt|salt]]\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Castor sugar|castor sugar]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| 1.5 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 4 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Peel the [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]]\n| Cut them in half lengthways and using a tablespoon or an [[Ice-cream scoop|ice-cream scoop]], remove the [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| Chop the [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] into 'moons', about 1cm [1/2 \" wide]\n| Toast the [[Sesame seeds|sesame seeds]] for a few minutes in a hot, dry pan so they turn golden\n| Put the [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] into a bowl and sprinkle with the [[Salt|salt]] then sit them in a [[Colander|colander]] for 10 minutes to allow them to drain\n| Rinse them under cold running water\n| Pat them dry with a [[Paper towel|paper towel]] or dry in a [[salad spinner]]\n| Add the [[Dried|dried]] [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] to a bowl and sprinkle with the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]] and [[Saute|saute]] the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]], the moment it start to color, remove from the heat, allow to cool then add it to the [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] and mix well\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe dressed with the [[Toasted sesame seeds|toasted sesame seeds]]\n===Variations===\nPartially peeling the [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] as in the picture make them really quite attractive.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cucumbers #oliveoil #cucumberandgarlicsalad #toastedsesameseeds #whitewinevinegar #peanutoil #saute #china #seeds #castorsugar #panfried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The salmon is livened up by using a spicy rub and then sealed in [[mayonnaise]] before is is oven baked, so all the moisture is retained.  It's then grilled to get a nice finish.\n\nWe regularly have [[Salmon|salmon]] and this may possibly be our recipe of choice.\n\nThanks to Julia for giving us permission to publish this recipe. fillets]] skin-side down on a sheet of [[Greaseproof paper|greaseproof paper]]\n| Add the rub ingredients to a small bowl and mix well\n| Sprinkle the rub over the top surface of the [[Salmon|salmon]], reserving a little to finish\n| Cover the [[Salmon|salmon]] [[Steak|steak]] with a thin layer of [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]]\n| Finish off with a sprinkle of the rub\n| Leaving the [[Salmon|salmon]] on the [[Greaseproof paper|greaseproof paper]], cover with a tent of [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]], being careful not to let the [[Foil|foil]] touch the [[Salmon|salmon]]\n| [[Bake]] for 20 minutes in the middle of the [[Oven|oven]].\n| When there is 5 minutes left, preheat the [[Grill|grill]]\n| After 20 minutes, finish under the [[Grill|grill]] for a few minutes\n}}\n<gallery ''Fried Chicken in Sweet Butter Sauce''.\n\nI have adapted this recipe to my taste and more easily available European ingredients from a now inactive Wikibooks recipe of the same name.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.3kg whole [[Chicken|chicken]], cut into small pieces ([[Jointing a chicken|see here]]) - also cut each breasts into 3 pieces\n| [[Oil]] for [[Frying|frying]] ([[Corn|corn]] oil, [[Rapeseed oil|rapeseed oil]], [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]] etc.)\n| [[Juice]] & [[Zest|zest]] from 1 [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| [[Juice]] and [[zest]] from 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| 2 teaspoons of fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n'''the [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n* 3 tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]]\n* 2 tablespoons of [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n* 2 tablespoons of light [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]]\n* 2 tablespoons of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n* 3 tablespoons [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]]\n* 2 tablespoons of [[Molasses|molasses]] or [[Black treacle|black treacle]]\n* 4 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and thinly sliced\n* 4 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n* 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and thinly sliced\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces to a bowl , add the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Citrus|citrus]] [[Zest|zest]] and juices and [[Marinate|marinate]] in the [[Refrigerator|refrigerator]] for at least a couple of hours. I usually leave them overnight.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]], pat the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces dry and and [[Fry|fry]] chicken until they are golden, drain on kitchen paper and set to one side.\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onion|onion]] for a a few minutes, then add the remaining [[Sauce|sauce]] ingredients.\n| [[Stir fry]] for a minute and then add [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces to reheat.\n| Serve with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]], garnished with slices of [[Lime|lime]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Plain boiled rice]], Slices of [[Lime|lime]] and a few chopped [[spring onions]].\n\n===Variations===\nFor a more authentic recipe:\n* Use [[Chinese cooking]] [[Wine|wine]] instead of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n* Use 8 tbsp Indonesian sweet soy sauce, [[kecap manis]] instead of [[dark soy sauce]] & [[molasses]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFor health reasons, I try to avoid frying whenever I can especially when there is already so much butter as in this recipe.  As a healthy alternative, I sprayed the chicken pieces with a little olive oil and roasted them for about 35 minutes at 220\u00b0C (425\u00b0, Gas 7).  They tasted just as nice!\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}} \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#friedchickeninsweetbuttersauce #chicken #zest #lime #onion #drysherry #darksoysauce #molasses #juice #garlic #plainboiledrice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Turn them often and be very careful not to burn them.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Plain rice|plain rice]] and garnish the [[Curry|curry]] with the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Coconut chips|coconut chips]] and [[Almonds|almonds]].\n===Variations===\nAny firm bodied [[Fish|fish]] would be fine; [[Cod|cod]], [[Haddock|haddock]], [[Mullet|mullet]] or even [[Prawns|prawns]].\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Olive oil]] is fine if you are keeping an eye on your [[cholesterol]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#almonds #fish #coconutchips #curry #raisins #coconutmilk #currypaste #pineapple #freeze #wok #plainrice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
